OBJECT Report 321 Vendor - Balance to Date
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=;
    Time=;
    Version List=NAVW19.00.00.45480,NAVSE9.00.00.45480;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    CaptionML=ENU=Vendor - Balance to Date;
    OnPreReport=BEGIN
                  VendFilter := Vendor.GETFILTERS;
                  VendDateFilter := Vendor.GETFILTER("Date Filter");
                END;

  }
  DATASET
  {
    { 3182;    ;DataItem;                    ;
               DataItemTable=Table23;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(No.);
               PrintOnlyIfDetail=Yes;
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               CurrReport.NEWPAGEPERRECORD := PrintOnePrPage;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  MaxDate := GETRANGEMAX("Date Filter");
                                  SETRANGE("Date Filter",0D,MaxDate);
                                  CALCFIELDS("Net Change (LCY)","Net Change","Inward Reg. Balance (LCY)");

                                  IF ((PrintAmountInLCY AND (Vendor."Net Change (LCY)" = 0) AND (Vendor."Inward Reg. Balance (LCY)" = 0)) OR
                                     ((NOT PrintAmountInLCY) AND (Vendor."Net Change" = 0) AND (Vendor."Inward Reg. Balance (LCY)" = 0)))
                                  THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=No.,Search Name,Blocked,Date Filter }

    { 2   ;1   ;Column  ;FORMAT_TODAY_0_4_   ;
               SourceExpr=FORMAT(TODAY,0,4) }

    { 3   ;1   ;Column  ;STRSUBSTNO_Text000_FORMAT_Vendor_GETRANGEMAX_;
               SourceExpr=STRSUBSTNO(Text000,FORMAT(Vendor.GETRANGEMAX("Date Filter"))) }

    { 6920;1   ;DataItem;VendLedgEntry3      ;
               DataItemTable=Table25;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Entry No.);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               RESET;
                               DtldVendLedgEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Vendor No.","Posting Date","Entry Type");
                               DtldVendLedgEntry.SETRANGE("Vendor No.",Vendor."No.");
                               DtldVendLedgEntry.SETRANGE("Entry Type",DtldVendLedgEntry."Entry Type"::Application);
                               IF NOT PrintUnappliedEntries  THEN
                                 DtldVendLedgEntry.SETRANGE(Unapplied,FALSE);

                               IF DtldVendLedgEntry.FIND('-') THEN
                                 REPEAT
                                   "Entry No." := DtldVendLedgEntry."Vendor Ledger Entry No.";
                                   MARK(TRUE);
                                 UNTIL DtldVendLedgEntry.NEXT = 0;

                               SETCURRENTKEY("Vendor No.",Open);
                               SETRANGE("Vendor No.",Vendor."No.");
                               SETRANGE(Open,TRUE);
                               SETRANGE("Posting Date",0D,MaxDate);
                               IF FIND('-') THEN
                                 REPEAT
                                   MARK(TRUE);
                                 UNTIL NEXT = 0;

                               SETCURRENTKEY("Entry No.");
                               SETRANGE(Open);
                               MARKEDONLY(TRUE);
                               SETRANGE("Date Filter",0D,MaxDate);

                               IF Vendor.GETFILTER("Global Dimension 1 Filter") <> '' THEN
                                 SETRANGE("Global Dimension 1 Code",Vendor.GETFILTER("Global Dimension 1 Filter"));
                               IF Vendor.GETFILTER("Global Dimension 2 Filter") <> '' THEN
                                 SETRANGE("Global Dimension 2 Code",Vendor.GETFILTER("Global Dimension 2 Filter"));
                               IF Vendor.GETFILTER("Currency Filter") <> '' THEN
                                 SETRANGE("Currency Code",Vendor.GETFILTER("Currency Filter"));
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF PrintAmountInLCY THEN BEGIN
                                    CALCFIELDS("Original Amt. (LCY)","Remaining Amt. (LCY)");
                                    OriginalAmt := "Original Amt. (LCY)";
                                    RemainingAmt := "Remaining Amt. (LCY)";
                                    CurrencyCode := '';
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                    CALCFIELDS("Original Amount","Remaining Amount");
                                    OriginalAmt := "Original Amount";
                                    RemainingAmt := "Remaining Amount";
                                    CurrencyCode := "Currency Code";
                                  END;

                                  IF RemainingAmt = 0 THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  CurrencyTotalBuffer.UpdateTotal(
                                    CurrencyCode,
                                    RemainingAmt,
                                    0,
                                    Counter1);
                                END;
                                 }

    { 28  ;2   ;Column  ;VendLedgEntry3__Posting_Date_;
               SourceExpr=FORMAT("Posting Date") }

    { 32  ;2   ;Column  ;VendLedgEntry3__Document_Type_;

    { 2149;2   ;DataItem;                    ;
               DataItemTable=Table380;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Vendor Ledger Entry No.,Posting Date)
                                 WHERE(Entry Type=FILTER(<>Initial Entry));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               DtldVendtLedgEntryNum := 0;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF NOT PrintUnappliedEntries  THEN
                                    IF Unapplied THEN
                                      CurrReport.SKIP;
                                  IF PrintAmountInLCY THEN BEGIN
                                    Amt := "Amount (LCY)";
                                    CurrencyCode := '';
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                    Amt := Amount;
                                    CurrencyCode := "Currency Code";
                                  END;
                                  IF Amt = 0 THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  DtldVendtLedgEntryNum := DtldVendtLedgEntryNum + 1;
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Vendor Ledger Entry No.=FIELD(Entry No.),
                            Posting Date=FIELD(Date Filter) }

    { 42  ;3   ;Column  ;Detailed_Vendor_Ledg__Entry__Entry_Type_;
               SourceExpr="Entry Type" }

    { 46  ;3   ;Column  ;Detailed_Vendor_Ledg__Entry__Posting_Date_;

    { 48  ;3   ;Column  ;Detailed_Vendor_Ledg__Entry__Document_Type_;

    { 52  ;3   ;Column  ;Amt                 ;

               AutoFormatType=1;

    { 56  ;3   ;Column  ;CurrencyCode_Control56;
               SourceExpr=CurrencyCode }

               SourceExpr=DtldVendtLedgEntryNum }

    { 13  ;3   ;Column  ;CurrencyCode_Control13;
               SourceExpr=CurrencyCode }

    { 11  ;3   ;Column  ;RemainingAmt        ;
               SourceExpr=RemainingAmt;
               AutoFormatType=1;
               AutoFormatExpr=CurrencyCode }

    { 39  ;3   ;Column  ;Detailed_Vendor_Ledg__Entry_Entry_No_;

    { 40  ;3   ;Column  ;Det_Vendor_Ledg__Entry_Vendor_Ledger_Entry_No_;
               SourceExpr="Vendor Ledger Entry No." }

    { 41  ;3   ;Column  ;Detailed_Vendor_Ledg__Entry_Posting_Date;
               SourceExpr="Posting Date" }

    { 6258;1   ;DataItem;<Inward Reg. Entry> ;
               DataItemTable=Table11128012;
               OnPreDataItem=VAR
                               AppliedInwardRegEntry@1070000 : Record 11128012;
                             BEGIN
                               SETCURRENTKEY("Vendor No.",Open);
                               SETRANGE("Vendor No.",Vendor."No.");
                               SETRANGE("Posting Date",0D,MaxDate);
                               IF FINDSET THEN
                                 REPEAT
                                   IF Open THEN
                                     MARK(TRUE)
                                   ELSE
                                     IF AppliedInwardRegEntry.GET("Applies-to Entry") THEN
                                       MARK(AppliedInwardRegEntry."Posting Date" > MaxDate);
                                 UNTIL NEXT = 0;

                               SETCURRENTKEY("Entry No.");
                               SETRANGE(Open);
                               MARKEDONLY(TRUE);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF NOT IncludeInwardReg THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;
                                  IF PrintAmountInLCY THEN BEGIN
                                    AmtInward := -"Amount Including VAT (LCY)";
                                    CurrencyCode := '';
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                    IF VATPostingSetup.GET("VAT Bus. Posting Group","VAT Prod. Posting Group") THEN BEGIN
                                      IF VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type" = VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT" THEN
                                        AmtInward := -Amount
                                      ELSE
                                        AmtInward := -(Amount + Amount * ("VAT %" / 100));
                                    END;
                                    CurrencyCode := "Currency Code";
                                  END;

                                  IF AmtInward = 0 THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  CurrencyTotalBuffer.UpdateTotal(
                                    CurrencyCode,
                                    AmtInward,
                                    0,
                                    Counter1);
                                END;
                                 }

    { 65  ;2   ;Column  ;Inward_Reg__PostingDate_;
               SourceExpr="Posting Date" }

    { 53  ;2   ;Column  ;Inward_Reg__Document_No__;
               SourceExpr="Document No." }

    { 66  ;2   ;Column  ;Inward_CurrencyCode ;
               SourceExpr=CurrencyCode }

    { 67  ;2   ;Column  ;AmtInward           ;
               SourceExpr=AmtInward }

    { 68  ;2   ;Column  ;Inward_Reg_Entry_Entry_No_;
               SourceExpr="Entry No." }

    { 4152;1   ;DataItem;Integer2            ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 WHERE(Number=FILTER(1..));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               CurrencyTotalBuffer.SETFILTER("Total Amount",'<>0');
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF Number = 1 THEN
                                    OK := CurrencyTotalBuffer.FIND('-')
                                  ELSE
                                    OK := CurrencyTotalBuffer.NEXT <> 0;
                                  IF NOT OK THEN
                                    CurrReport.BREAK;

                                  CurrencyTotalBuffer2.UpdateTotal(
                                    CurrencyTotalBuffer."Currency Code",
                                    CurrencyTotalBuffer."Total Amount",
                                    0,
                                    Counter1);
                                END;

               OnPostDataItem=BEGIN
                                CurrencyTotalBuffer.DELETEALL;
                              END;
                               }

    { 9   ;2   ;Column  ;Vendor_Name_Control9;
               SourceExpr=Vendor.Name }

    { 98  ;2   ;Column  ;CurrencyTotalBuffer__Total_Amount_;

    { 7913;    ;DataItem;Integer3            ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 WHERE(Number=FILTER(1..));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               CurrencyTotalBuffer2.SETFILTER("Total Amount",'<>0');
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF Number = 1 THEN
                                    OK := CurrencyTotalBuffer2.FIND('-')
                                  ELSE
                                    OK := CurrencyTotalBuffer2.NEXT <> 0;
                                  IF NOT OK THEN
                                    CurrReport.BREAK;
                                END;

               OnPostDataItem=BEGIN
                                CurrencyTotalBuffer2.DELETEALL;
                              END;
                               }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
